Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Comanche 45/2 (AKA Manche45 revision 2), the final, flown mission release of the Apollo 10 Command Module (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software. Comanche 45/2 was preceded by Comanche 44 and Comanche 45. The reconstruction is believed to be exactly accurate, but in the absence of an actual Apollo-era listing of Comanche 45/2, some explanation of the reconstruction process is needed to insure confidence in that accuracy.

The starting point was the source code of Comanche 45 (itself previously accurately reconstructed). Comanche 45 source code was then modified by incorporating changes known from contemporary documentation to have been made between revisions 45 and 45/2. The now-reconstructed Comanche 45/2 source code was verified by assembling it and checking that the assembled code had the expected known-correct memory-bank checksums. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code tend to match those in the Comanche 55, the most-similar revision of Comanche for which we have access to an actual non-reconstructed hardcopy; the source code would likely have different page numbers in a contemporary Comanche 45 listing.

Annotations that were not present in the contemporary source code have been added to the reconstructed code to justify each change relative to Comanche 44. Here's a guide to the Apollo documentation referenced in those annotations:
  • MIT/IL engineering drawing 2021153D, sheet 3. Listing of the memory-bank checksums for Comanche 45.
  • Reconstructed Comanche 45 (Apollo 10 CM second release) assembly listing.
  • Reconstructed Comanche 51 (Apollo 11 CM initial release) assembly listing.
  • Programmed Guidance Equations for Colossus 2, p. 91.
Comments expected to have been present in the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC Project's GitHub repository. 

012916,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
012917,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
012918,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Manche45 revision 2.
012919,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the
012920,000006:                                                                                                  ##              final, flown release of the flight software for the Command
012921,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 10.
012922,000008:                                                                                                  ##              The code has been recreated from a copy of Comanche 055. It
012923,000009:                                                                                                  ##              has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
012924,000010:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Manche 45/2 in NASA drawing
012925,000011:                                                                                                  ##              2021153D, which gives relatively high confidence that the
012926,000012:                                                                                                  ##              reconstruction is correct.
012927,000013:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
012928,000014:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
012929,000015:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
012930,000016:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2020-12-24 MAS  Created from Comanche 45.
012931,000017:

012933,000019:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
012934,000020:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDISK REV 17
012935,000021:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
012936,000022:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
012937,000023: 
012938,000024:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
012939,000025: 
012940,000026:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
012941,000027:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
012942,000028:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
012943,000029:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
012944,000030: 
012945,000031:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
012946,000032:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
012947,000033:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
012948,000034:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
012949,000035:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
012950,000036: 
012951,000037:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
012952,000038:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
012953,000039:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
012954,000040:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
012955,000041: 
012956,000042:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
012957,000043:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
012958,000044: 
012959,000045:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
012960,000046: 
012961,000047:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
012962,000048:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A MAIN (NAVIGATION) KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES
012963,000049:                                                                                                  #  INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO 
012964,000050:                                                                                                  #  CHANNEL 15 (CHANNEL 16).  KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) PLACES THE KEY
012965,000051:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
012966,000052:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012967,000053: 
012968,000054:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
012969,000055:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
012970,000056:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
012971,000057:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012972,000058: 
012973,000059:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
012974,000060:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
012975,000061:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
012976,000062:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
012977,000063:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
012978,000064: 
012979,000065:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
012980,000066: 
012981,000067:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
012982,000068:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.

Page 308 

012984,000070:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
012985,000071:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
012986,000072:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
012987,000073:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
012988,000074:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
012989,000075:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
012990,000076:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
012991,000077:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
012992,000078:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
012993,000079:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
012994,000080:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
012995,000081: 
012996,000082:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
012997,000083:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
012998,000084:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
012999,000085: 
013000,000086:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
013001,000087: 
013002,000088:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
013003,000089:                                                                                                  #                IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
013004,000090:                                                                                                  #                ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
013005,000091: 
013006,000092:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
013007,000093:                                                                                                  #                IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
013008,000094:                                                                                                  #                (WITH OCTAL 01501).
013009,000095:                                                                                                  #                IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
013010,000096:                                                                                                  #                CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206).  THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
013011,000097:                                                                                                  #                1)      ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
013012,000098:                                                                                                  #                2)      NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
013013,000099: 
013014,000100:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
013015,000101:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
013016,000102: 
013017,000103:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
013018,000104: 
013019,000105:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
013020,000106:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
013021,000107:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
013022,000108:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
013023,000109: 
013024,000110:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
013025,000111: 
013026,000112:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
013027,000113:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
013028,000114:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
013029,000115:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
013030,000116:

Page 309 

013032,000118:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
013033,000119:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
013034,000120: 
013035,000121:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
013036,000122: 
013037,000123:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
013038,000124:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
013039,000125: 
013040,000126:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
013041,000127:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
013042,000128:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
013043,000129:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
013044,000130: 
013045,000131:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
013046,000132:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
013047,000133: 
013048,000134:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
013049,000135:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
013050,000136:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
013051,000137:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
013052,000138: 
013053,000139:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
013054,000140:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
013055,000141: 
013056,000142:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
013057,000143:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V33) FUNCTION.
013058,000144: 
013059,000145:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
013060,000146: 
013061,000147:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
013062,000148:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
013063,000149:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
013064,000150:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013065,000151: 
013066,000152:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
013067,000153:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013068,000154: 
013069,000155:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
013070,000156:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
013071,000157: 
013072,000158:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
013073,000159:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
013074,000160:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.

(Note that this doc by Green and Filene is/was available online at http://hrst.mit.edu/hrs/apollo/public/archive/1706.pdf — RSB 6/2004.)

013090,000176:                                                                                                  # DSPCOUNT       ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
013091,000177:                                                                                                  # DECBRNCH       ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
013092,000178:                                                                                                  # VERBREG        ERASE                   VERB CODE
013093,000179:                                                                                                  # NOUNREG        ERASE                   NOUN CODE
013094,000180:                                                                                                  # XREG           ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
013095,000181:                                                                                                  # YREG           ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
013096,000182:                                                                                                  # ZREG           ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
013097,000183:                                                                                                  # XREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013098,000184:                                                                                                  # YREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013099,000185:                                                                                                  # HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013100,000186:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
013101,000187:                                                                                                  # ZREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013102,000188:                                                                                                  # LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013103,000189:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
013104,000190:                                                                                                  # MODREG         ERASE                   MODE CODE
013105,000191:                                                                                                  # DSPLOCK        ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
013106,000192:                                                                                                  # REQRET         ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
013107,000193:                                                                                                  # LOADSTAT       ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
013108,000194:                                                                                                  # CLPASS         ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
013109,000195:                                                                                                  # NOUT           ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
013110,000196:                                                                                                  # NOUNCADR       ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
013111,000197:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE        ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
013112,000198:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE1       ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR(MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
013113,000199:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE2       ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
013114,000200:                                                                                                  # DSPTAB         ERASE   +13D            0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER. 11-13, C RELAYS
013115,000201:                                                                                                  # CADRSTOR       ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
013116,000202:                                                                                                  # NVQTEM         ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
013117,000203:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
013118,000204:                                                                                                  # NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
013119,000205:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
013120,000206:                                                                                                  # VERBSAVE       ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
013121,000207:                                                                                                  # DSPLIST        ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
013122,000208:                                                                                                  # EXTVBACT       REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
013123,000209:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM1        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
013124,000210:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM2        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
013125,000211:

013192,000278: 
013193,000279:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
013194,000280:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
013195,000281:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
013196,000282:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
013197,000283:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
013198,000284: 
013199,000285:                                                                                                  #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
013200,000286: 
013201,000287:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013202,000288: 
013203,000289:                                                                                                  # DSPCNT         ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
013204,000290:                                                                                                  # UPLOCK         ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
013205,000291:                                                                                                  #                                        RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
013206,000292: 
013207,000293:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013208,000294: 
013209,000295:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013210,000296: 
013211,000297:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP1       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013212,000298:                                                                                                  # DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
013213,000299:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP2       =       RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013214,000300: 
013215,000301:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013216,000302:

Page 313 

013218,000304:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
013219,000305:                                                                                                  #        0               10000
013220,000306:                                                                                                  #        1               00001
013221,000307:                                                                                                  #        9               01001
013222,000308:                                                                                                  #        VERB            10001
013223,000309:                                                                                                  #        ERROR RES       10010
013224,000310:                                                                                                  #        KEY RLSE        11001
013225,000311:                                                                                                  #        +               11010
013226,000312:                                                                                                  #        -               11011
013227,000313:                                                                                                  #        ENTER           11100
013228,000314:                                                                                                  #        CLEAR           11110
013229,000315:                                                                                                  #        NOUN            11111
013230,000316: 
013231,000317:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
013232,000318:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD.  THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
013233,000319:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
013234,000320:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
013235,000321:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
013236,000322:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
013237,000323: 
013238,000324:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
013239,000325:                                                                                                  #        MD1             MD2 (MAJOR MODE)
013240,000326:                                                                                                  #        VD1             VD2 (VERB)                      ND1             ND2 (NOUN)
013241,000327:                                                                                                  #        R1D1            R1D2            R1D3            R1D4            R1D5 (R1)
013242,000328:                                                                                                  #        R2D1            R2D2            R2D3            R2D4            R2D5 (R2)
013243,000329:                                                                                                  #        R3D1            R3D2            R3D3            R3D4            R3D5 (R3)
013244,000330: 
013245,000331:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
013246,000332: 
013247,000333:                                                                                                  #        MD1     25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
013248,000334:                                                                                                  #        MD2     24              R2D2    10
013249,000335:                                                                                                  #        VD1     23              R2D3    7
013250,000336:                                                                                                  #        VD2     22              R2D4    6
013251,000337:                                                                                                  #        ND1     21              R2D5    5
013252,000338:                                                                                                  #        ND2     20              R3D1    4
013253,000339:                                                                                                  #        R1D1    16              R3D2    3
013254,000340:                                                                                                  #        R1D2    15              R3D3    2
013255,000341:                                                                                                  #        R1D3    14              R3D4    1
013256,000342:                                                                                                  #        R1D4    13              R3D5    0
013257,000343:                                                                                                  #        R1D5    12
013258,000344: 
013259,000345:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
013260,000346: 
013261,000347:                                                                                                  #        DSPTAB          RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
013262,000348:                                                                                                  #        RELADD
013263,000349:                                                                                                  #        10              1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2  (24)
013264,000350:                                                                                                  #        9               1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2  (22)
013265,000351:                                                                                                  #        8               1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2  (20)
013266,000352:                                                                                                  #        7               1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 314 

013268,000354:                                                                                                  #        6               0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
013269,000355:                                                                                                  #        5               0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
013270,000356:                                                                                                  #        4               0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
013271,000357:                                                                                                  #        3               0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
013272,000358:                                                                                                  #        2               0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
013273,000359:                                                                                                  #        1               0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
013274,000360:                                                                                                  #        0               0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
013275,000361:                                                                                                  #                        0000        NO RELAYWORD
013276,000362: 
013277,000363:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
013278,000364: 
013279,000365:                                                                                                  #        BLANK   00000
013280,000366:                                                                                                  #        0       10101
013281,000367:                                                                                                  #        1       00011
013282,000368:                                                                                                  #        2       11001
013283,000369:                                                                                                  #        3       11011
013284,000370:                                                                                                  #        4       01111
013285,000371:                                                                                                  #        5       11110
013286,000372:                                                                                                  #        6       11100
013287,000373:                                                                                                  #        7       10011
013288,000374:                                                                                                  #        8       11101
013289,000375:                                                                                                  #        9       11111
013290,000376: 
013291,000377:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
013292,000378: 
013293,000379:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
013294,000380:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
013295,000381:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
013296,000382:

013695,000781:                                                                                                  #  ENTER PASS 0 IS THE EXECUTE FUNCTION.  HIGHER ORDER ENTERS ARE TO LOAD
013696,000782:                                                                                                  #  DATA.  THE SIGN OF REQRET DETERMINES THE PASS, + FOR PASS 0, - FOR HIGHER
013697,000783:                                                                                                  #  PASSES.
013698,000784: 
013699,000785:                                                                                                  #  MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED (MCTBS) NOUNS DESIRE AN ECADR TO BE LOADED

Page 330 

013987,001073:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
013988,001074: 
013989,001075:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
013990,001076:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE ECADR FOR EACH NOUN.
013991,001077:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.  - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
013992,001078:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED.  -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
013993,001079:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
013994,001080: 
013995,001081:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
013996,001082:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
013997,001083: 
013998,001084:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
013999,001085: 
014000,001086:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
014001,001087:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
014002,001088:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
014003,001089: 
014004,001090:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
014005,001091:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
014006,001092:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
014007,001093:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
014008,001094:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
014009,001095:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
014010,001096: 
014011,001097:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
014012,001098:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.  IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
014013,001099:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
014014,001100: 
014015,001101:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
014016,001102:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
014017,001103: 
014018,001104:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
014019,001105:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
014020,001106: 
014021,001107:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
014022,001108: 
014023,001109:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
014024,001110:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
014025,001111:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014026,001112:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
014027,001113:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014028,001114: 
014029,001115:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
014030,001116:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
014031,001117:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
014032,001118: 
014033,001119:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
014034,001120:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED.  ALARM IF VIOLATION.
014035,001121: 
014036,001122:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
014037,001123:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER.  IF NOT, ALARM.
014038,001124:

Page 331 

014040,001126:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS

014562,001648:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.

Page 355 

015168,002254:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY.  IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
015169,002255:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
015170,002256:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
015171,002257:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
015172,002258:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
015173,002259: 
015174,002260:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
015175,002261:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.  IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
015176,002262:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE.  IT SAVES
015177,002263:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  BIT 15 OF
015178,002264:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT).  BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
015179,002265:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
015180,002266:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT).  IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
015181,002267: 
015182,002268:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
015183,002269:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015184,002270:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015185,002271: 
015186,002272:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
015187,002273:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
015188,002274: 
015189,002275:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
015190,002276:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
015191,002277: 
015192,002278:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW
015193,002279: 
015194,002280: 41,3230                                           SETLOC   ENDRUTIN

015321,002407: 
015322,002408:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
015323,002409:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  THE FCADR OF THE 
015324,002410:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN.  IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
015325,002411:                                                                                                  #  
015326,002412:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
015327,002413: 
015328,002414:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
015329,002415:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
015330,002416:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
015331,002417: 
015332,002418:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
015333,002419:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
015334,002420:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
015335,002421: 
015336,002422: 41,3353           34333        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
015337,002423: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
015338,002424: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
015339,002425: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
015340,002426: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
015341,002427: 41,3360           04715                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
015342,002428: 41,3361           03363                           TC       DSPOCTWD

015765,002851:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.

Page 368 

015767,002853: 
015768,002854:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
015769,002855: 
015770,002856:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
015771,002857: 
015772,002858:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
015773,002859:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
015774,002860:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
015775,002861:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
015776,002862: 
015777,002863:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
015778,002864:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
015779,002865:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
015780,002866: 
015781,002867:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
015782,002868:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
015783,002869:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
015784,002870:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
015785,002871:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
015786,002872:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
015787,002873:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES.  HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
015788,002874:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
015789,002875:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
015790,002876:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
015791,002877:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
015792,002878: 
015793,002879: 40,3366           45015        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
015794,002880: 40,3367           00006                           EXTEND                                         
015795,002881: 40,3370           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
015796,002882: 40,3371           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
015797,002883: 40,3372           35002                           CAF      BIT14                                 
015798,002884: 40,3373           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
015799,002885: 40,3374           10000                           CCS      A                                     
015800,002886: 40,3375           03404                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
015801,002887: 40,3376           04473        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
015802,002888: 40,3377           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
015803,002889: 40,3400           03402                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
015804,002890: 40,3401           05217                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015805,002891: 40,3402           04701                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
015806,002892: 40,3403           21272                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
015807,002893: 40,3404           35021        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
015808,002894: 40,3405           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
015809,002895: 40,3406           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
015810,002896: 40,3407           05217                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
015811,002897: 40,3410           04516                           TC       RELDSP1                               
015812,002898: 40,3411           05217                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015813,002899: 
015814,002900: 40,3412                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
015815,002901:

Page 369 

015817,002903:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER.  IT CAN BE
015818,002904:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
015819,002905:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
015820,002906:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
015821,002907:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
015822,002908: 
015823,002909:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
015824,002910:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
015825,002911:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
015826,002912: 
015827,002913:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
015828,002914:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
015829,002915: 
015830,002916:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015831,002917:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE.  THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
015832,002918:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
015833,002919:                                                                                                  #  ACTION).  IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
015834,002920:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
015835,002921: 
015836,002922:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015837,002923:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
015838,002924:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
015839,002925:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
015840,002926: 
015841,002927:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
015842,002928:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
015843,002929:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
015844,002930:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
015845,002931:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
015846,002932:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
015847,002933:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
015848,002934: 
015849,002935:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
015850,002936:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
015851,002937: 
015852,002938:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
015853,002939:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
015854,002940: 
015855,002941:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
015856,002942:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
015857,002943: 
015858,002944:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
015859,002945:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
015860,002946:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
015861,002947:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
015862,002948:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
015863,002949:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS.  THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
015864,002950:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
015865,002951: 
015866,002952:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 370 

015868,002954:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
015869,002955:                                                                                                  #  A.  AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
015870,002956:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
015871,002957:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L.  IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
015872,002958:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS.  (THIS VERB
015873,002959:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
015874,002960:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
015875,002961:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
015876,002962:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
015877,002963: 
015878,002964:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
015879,002965:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET.  (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)

015989,003075:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).
015990,003076: 
015991,003077:    4220                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
015992,003078:    4220                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
015993,003079:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
015994,003080:    4220           35001        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
015995,003081:    4221           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
015996,003082:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
015997,003083:    4222           00002                           TC       Q                                     
015998,003084: 
015999,003085:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA).  SET BY NVSUB
016000,003086:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016001,003087:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE       SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016002,003088:                                                                                                  #                -0      DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
016003,003089:                                                                                                  #                        OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
016004,003090: 
016005,003091:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
016006,003092:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
016007,003093:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED.  ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
016008,003094:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016009,003095:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016010,003096:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
016011,003097:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
016012,003098:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
016013,003099:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
016014,003100:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.

Page 373 

016016,003102: 
016017,003103:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
016018,003104:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
016019,003105:                                                                                                  #        1)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
016020,003106:                                                                                                  #                EXCEEDED.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016021,003107:                                                                                                  #        2)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
016022,003108:                                                                                                  #                NVSUBUSY.
016023,003109: 
016024,003110:    4223           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
016025,003111:    4224           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
016026,003112:    4225           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
016027,003113:    4226           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
016028,003114:    4227           75054                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
016029,003115:    4230           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
016030,003116:    4231           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR

016032,003118:
