016186,003272:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED), TERMINATE VERB IS EXECUTED, OR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA VERB IS
016187,003273:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED.  IT WAKES UP JOB THAT DID TC ENDIDLE.

016189,003275:                                                                                                  #  IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0, IT PUTS +0 INTO DSPLOCK, AND TURNS OFF KEY RLSE
016190,003276:                                                                                                  #  LIGHT IF DSPLIST IS EMPTY (LEAVES KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE IF NOT EMPTY).

Page 381 

016366,003452:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016367,003453: 
016368,003454:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
016369,003455:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR.  THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
016370,003456:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
016371,003457:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
016372,003458: 
016373,003459:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016374,003460:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1)      BY ENDIDLE
016375,003461:                                                                                                  #                2)      BY NVSUBUSY
016376,003462:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
016377,003463:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME.  IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016378,003464:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY AJOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
016379,003465:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
016380,003466: 
016381,003467:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
016382,003468:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
016383,003469:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
016384,003470:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
016385,003471:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
016386,003472: 
016387,003473:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
016388,003474:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016389,003475:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM.  NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
016390,003476:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016391,003477:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016392,003478: 
016393,003479:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
016394,003480:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
016395,003481:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
016396,003482:                                                                                                  #  .
016397,003483: 
016398,003484:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
016399,003485:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION).  IT IS
016400,003486:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
016401,003487:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
016402,003488: 
016403,003489:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016404,003490:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
016405,003491:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
016406,003492: 
016407,003493:                                                                                                  #        1)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
016408,003494:                                                                                                  #                IS EXCEEDED.
016409,003495:                                                                                                  #        2)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 382 

016411,003497:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016412,003498: 
016413,003499:    4453           44460        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
016414,003500:    4454           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
016415,003501:    4455           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
016416,003502:    4456           04701        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
016417,003503:    4457           10577                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
016418,003504:    4460           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
016419,003505: 
016420,003506:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
016421,003507:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
016422,003508: 
016423,003509: 04,2577                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
016424,003510: 04,2577                                           COUNT    07/PIN                                
016425,003511: 
016426,003512: 04,2577           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
016427,003513: 04,2600           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
016428,003514: 04,2601           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
016429,003515: 04,2602           04410                           TC       RELDSPON                              
016430,003516: 04,2603           30001                           CA       L                                     
016431,003517: 04,2604           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
016432,003518: 04,2605           05175        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016433,003519: 
016434,003520:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
016435,003521:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
016436,003522:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE).  IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
016437,003523:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
016438,003524:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
016439,003525: 
016440,003526:    4461                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
016441,003527:    4461                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
016442,003528: 
016443,003529:    4461           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016444,003530:    4462           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
016445,003531:    4463           35002                           CAF      BIT14                                 
016446,003532:    4464           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016447,003533:    4465           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
016448,003534:    4466           10000                           CCS      A                                     
016449,003535:    4467           14471                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
016450,003536:    4470           14200                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
016451,003537:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
016452,003538:    4471           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2.  PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
016453,003539:    4472           14453                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
016454,003540: 
016455,003541:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
016456,003542:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
016457,003543: 
016458,003544:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
016459,003545: 
016460,003546:    4473           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT

Page 383 

016462,003548:    4474           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST

016602,003688:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
